[30;1m476 | [0m[35med with resetting an async FIFO - Gray code counters which[0m
[30;1m477 | [0m[35m        # are reset to 0 violate their Gray code invariant. One way to handle this is to ensure[0m
[30;1m478 | [0m[35m        # that both sides of the FIFO are asynchronously reset by the same signal. We adopt a[0m
[30;1m479 | [0m[35m        # slight variation on this approach - reset control rests entirely with the write domain.[0m
[30;1m480 | [0m[35m        # The write domain's reset signal is used to asynchronously reset the read domain's[0m
